.cd-headline.rotate-1 b.is-hidden { transform: rotateX(180deg); animation: 1.2s ease 0s 1 normal none running cd-rotate-1-out; }

  65% { opacity: 0; }
  100% { transform: rotateX(360deg); opacity: 1; }
}

}

}

  100% { transform: rotateX(180deg); opacity: 0; }
}
